I get the Nigiri combo every time - miso, salad 5 piece assorted sushi + 6 piece cut roll

Don‚Äôt come to this restaurant if you want: California rolls, spicy tuna, eel sauce, spicy mayo, tempura etc. This is traditional Japanese sushi, come for the fish.

<Review>Incredibly amazing! Hands down THE BEST and is now MY favorite sushi restaurant in LA.

Having Sushi Sushi bookmarked for quite awhile now; co workers and I were able to clear our schedule and come in for lunch.

Sushi Sushi is located on Beverly Dr. in the city of Beverly Hills. Traffic is always heavy and parking can be a pain. Lucky for us we came right before the lunch crowd and scored a metered spot across from the restaurant. Meter accepts coins and credit cards!

The restaurant is very traditional and has that Japanese authentic feel. Warm towels were given at the beginning and end of our meal.

The premium sushi combo ($24) is the best deal on their menu and served only during lunch.
The premium sushi combo comes with a shitake mushroom miso, salad with pieces of fresh mackerel, 8 pieces of sushi and a toro cut roll. The 8 pieces are chef's choice so it changes daily. I was glad mine came with toro, sweet shrimp, and eel.

The quality of the fish was outstanding. Service was impeccable. No complaints at all.

I'm now a fan! Thank you!< /Review>< pics>

<user>109749011333697186307</user>< Name>
Desiree Parsons</Name>
<Time>1408387819033< /Time><Rate>4< /Rate>< Review>
There is no question to the quality of cakes or design skills at Michelle's. These are European style cakes, so they are decadent, dense, and moist. The flavors are unique and the quality of these cakes are miles above the competition in my opinion. I've had the pleasure of tasting cakes from some of the biggest named bakeries in LA, OC, and NY in my past days working in the wedding business and to me none really have rivaled Michelle's. The "Victorian" variety of cakes and triple chocolate cake are truly superb. They are the work of a true master pastry chef and when you consider the prices there really isn't a better choice to be made. The ONLY reason I cannot give 5 stars pertains to the customer service. I've had no problems personally with Michelle's mother but it is evident that one must tread lightly around her. Michelle herself is delightful but I have witnessed the cross, rude manner of her mother directly with other clients on more than one occasion in my many visits to this bakery. I have not seen this affect the bakery's ability to meet the demands of their business so I can see why many people continue to patron Michelle's in spite of many poor customer service reviews. I will always recommend this bakery and simply warn people not to be put off by the not-so-friendly woman manning the phone and counter. However my personal opinion is that there is no room for ungracious, impolite behavior in the wedding industry. For many women it's the one and only time in their lives that they get to feel like the a super special and important person and they should be treated as such.   I would not be surprised to learn that Michelle's is flourishing in spite of poor customer service because the quality of her cakes sell themselves. I do believe her business could skyrocket though with a little warmth and gratitude coming from the front of the house where mom appears to run the show.<//Review>

<text>In the world of high end jewelry/watch shopping there's Davidson and Licht and then there's everyone else. From the moment the door is opened for you by a dapper gentleman who smiles and calls your attention to the hand sanitizer, to the champagne/scotch (or chilled bottled water if you prefer) and candied orange slices. This place is pure class without the pretentiousness which usually accompanies multi-million dollar jewelry caches and Rolex/Cartier Authorized Dealer status.

My wife and I spent at least two hours (probably closer to three) poring over various Rolex, Cartier and IWC watches and truly extravagant jewelry. Not once did we feel pressured to purchase. Not once did we encounter the "slickness" all too familiar in high end sales salons. What we did feel was supported and guided through our decision making process. To that end, we owe particular thanks to Orlando, his expertise and his patience. Aside from being a genuine and convivial fellow, it was clearly important to Orlando that our purchase was the right purchase for us. No pressure. No undue urgency tactics. He simply used his knowledge and experience to educate us about what we might like the most and let our preferences lead us from there. Thank you Orlando and thank you Davidson and Licht for a magnificent shopping experience!< /text><pics>None< /pics>< Resp>

You can look through the scope and see how perfectly symmetrical the diamonds are. They are the best cut diamonds in the world, and "Cut" is the most important of the four C's. I was drawn to the 1ct. pair and tried them on. I was sold.
The next day I came back and Vince immediately greeted me again. I wanted to be sure I made the right choice. I tried on a larger more expensive pair and he said they both work but the smaller ones are perfect for everyday wear. He suggested I keep the ones I got. I really appreciated that he didn't up-sell me. Turns out they don't work on commission, how amazing is that; I feel like I can breath unlike at other jewelry stores. Vince made great conversation during the whole experience. He offered to appraise the alexandrite ring I brought in for free. < Review>
My wife and I have always been treated well here, even when we were "just looking". We bought a Rolex a number of years ago at their other Walnut Creek location. A few weeks ago we needed to have the band adjusted so we came back. To our surprise it wasn't there. We googled it and walked to the new location.

The new store is beautiful! We walked in with jeans and tennis shoes. We were immediately greeted and helped. While we waited we looked at their large selection of Rolexes. We met Jon Licht, the owner and Jeremiah, the in-house Rolex expert. We learned so much from him about the history of Rolex. Jon has a great sense of humor and gift of gab. We bought two Rolexes! While we were looking they offered to clean our rings and our watches. They cleaned and polished them for free.

We spoke with Jon about our 25th anniversary next year and our desire to have rings made for the special occasion. He put a $100K ring on my wife and walked away. Then I wore it walking around the store. When Jon came back we discussed different possible designs.

We were treated as if we were part of his family. We were not dressed well. We were not wearing a lot of expensive jewelry. We are gay. Sometimes other stores do not give us the time of day, so we just leave and find another store who will treat us with respect. We did not feel this way any time we entered this store.

I highly recommend shopping here.</Review>
